# Name & Place Variant Spellings Across Witness Translations

Generated by `scripts/33_name_variants.py` (roadmap Phase 5: "Create a list of all locations and names and any variances of those names in other translations").

For each KJV proper noun (script 05 heuristic, Decision Log #7), capitalized tokens in the same verse of each English witness with spelling similarity >= 0.72 but a different spelling are listed as variants. **Advisory only** (Premise Revision): these feed the Decision Log #7 name-retranslation research (e.g. Agar → Hagar); matching is heuristic, so entries may include near-name noise — owner review applies before any use in restorations.

Names with at least one variant: **2846** of 3503 proper-noun forms.
